EU pozivi za MSP iz Srbije, Malte i Slovenije

EU cascade funding F6S / AID4SME Horizon Europe project score 18

AID4SME Open Call #2

Horizon Europe cascade funding call for SMEs and startups developing AI and data-driven solutions for industrial resource optimisation and Green Deal challenges. Offers up to EUR 200,000 per project, equity-free, for up to 12 projects. Official FAQ states eligible Horizon Europe associated countries can apply; Serbian SMEs should verify against the latest Horizon Europe associated-country list and the applicant guidelines.

Rok
2026-07-15
Status
open
Ruta
Serbia / Western Balkans
Kljucne reci
ai, cascade funding, data, f6s, grant, green deal, horizon europe, serbia potential, sme, startup
Apply

Najverovatnije aplicira srpska firma ili konzorcijum sa Srbijom. Proveri status Srbije u konkretnom programu.

1. Firma i eligibility

  • Company registration extract: APR for Serbia, MBR for Malta, or equivalent register
  • SME declaration: employees, turnover, balance sheet total, linked/partner enterprises
  • Ownership and UBO structure, with authorised representative details
  • Tax ID, VAT number if applicable, bank account confirmation
  • Short company profile and reference projects
  • Complete F6S company and founder profiles
  • Decide lead applicant: Serbia, Malta or Slovenia SME/startup
  • Confirm one-application-per-entity rule before using multiple companies

2. Projekat

  • One-page project concept: problem, solution, target users, expected result
  • Work plan with work packages, milestones, deliverables and timeline
  • Market and impact section: customers, traction, benefits and KPIs
  • Team CVs for key people and role allocation
  • Risk table: technical, commercial, regulatory and delivery risks
  • Short F6S application answers with clear pilot use case
  • Select exactly one AID4SME challenge code and align every section to it
  • Write the Annex 2 proposal in the mandatory AID4SME template
  • Define 14-month plan: Plan, Development, Testing & Validation, Assessment
  • Define mandatory deliverables: IP Agreement by M4, Test & Validation Report by M10, Business Plan and Exploitation Roadmap by M14

3. Budzet i finansije

  • Detailed budget by partner and cost category
  • Supplier quotes or cost assumptions for equipment, services and subcontracting
  • Latest financial statements, management accounts or balance sheet
  • State-aid, de minimis and double-funding declarations where requested
  • Cash-flow plan for pre-financing and co-financing
  • Budget for 70% funding rate and maximum EUR 200,000 contribution
  • No subcontracting: keep external work out of the requested project costs
  • Use depreciation only for equipment costs during the project period

4. Partneri i podnosenje

  • Official call text and applicant guide saved locally
  • Eligibility checklist completed before writing the full proposal
  • Authorised signatory decision or power of attorney
  • Submission portal account: EU Login, F6S, national portal or programme portal
  • Final PDF/application package and proof of submission
  • F6S application workspace access for all contributors
  • Upload final Annex 2 proposal PDF through F6S only
  • Prepare Declaration of Honour, SME Declaration and consortium declaration for contracting if selected
  • Submit before 15 July 2026, 17:00 CEST; do not wait for the final hour
Otvori zvanicni poziv
UK ARPA-style frontier R&D ARIA score 10

ARIA Trust Everything, Everywhere: Opportunity seeds

Open UK ARIA opportunity seed call for cyber-physical trust infrastructure, with funding available up to GBP 500,000 per project. This is a frontier R&D route rather than a standard SME grant; use it if the solution has a high-risk technical angle in software/hardware trust, security, AI assurance or cyber-physical markets. Check ARIA applicant guidance for non-UK team eligibility and UK benefit requirements before applying.

EU cascade funding OpenCalls.fund / Reframe Food score 12

LIGAWINE Open Call

EU-funded FSTP open call for sustainability, climate resilience and competitiveness in the European wine sector. Supports technology providers and wineries through testing, adaptation and validation of low-input, environmentally friendly and digitally enabled innovations. Potentially relevant to Serbian wineries/tech providers; eligibility should be checked in the applicants guide before applying.

Rok
2026-07-31
Status
open
Ruta
EU agrifood cascade route
Kljucne reci
cascade funding, climate resilience, fstp, grant, sme potential, wine sector
Apply

Ovo je FSTP/cascade agrifood ruta. Treba brzo naci use-case partnera: winery, food business, innovation hub, farmer/producer ili regional cluster.

1. Firma i eligibility

  • Company registration extract: APR for Serbia, MBR for Malta, or equivalent register
  • SME declaration: employees, turnover, balance sheet total, linked/partner enterprises
  • Ownership and UBO structure, with authorised representative details
  • Tax ID, VAT number if applicable, bank account confirmation
  • Short company profile and reference projects
  • Agrifood/winery/food-safety sector fit and SME or innovation-hub eligibility evidence

2. Projekat

  • One-page project concept: problem, solution, target users, expected result
  • Work plan with work packages, milestones, deliverables and timeline
  • Market and impact section: customers, traction, benefits and KPIs
  • Team CVs for key people and role allocation
  • Risk table: technical, commercial, regulatory and delivery risks
  • Use-case partner description: winery, food business, innovation hub, producer, farmer or regional cluster
  • Pilot plan for testing, validation, mentoring, training or deployment in a real food/agri environment
  • Sustainability and digital-enablement angle: low inputs, traceability, safety, resource efficiency or decision support
  • Quantified environmental or climate impact baseline and target KPIs
  • Pilot/demo site description and permitting or regulatory assumptions
  • Replication and exploitation plan for EU markets

3. Budzet i finansije

  • Detailed budget by partner and cost category
  • Supplier quotes or cost assumptions for equipment, services and subcontracting
  • Latest financial statements, management accounts or balance sheet
  • State-aid, de minimis and double-funding declarations where requested
  • Cash-flow plan for pre-financing and co-financing
  • FSTP budget template with eligible staff, travel, pilot, equipment/service and subcontracting assumptions
  • Co-financing plan, capital-expenditure assumptions and eligible-cost split

4. Partneri i podnosenje

  • Official call text and applicant guide saved locally
  • Eligibility checklist completed before writing the full proposal
  • Authorised signatory decision or power of attorney
  • Submission portal account: EU Login, F6S, national portal or programme portal
  • Final PDF/application package and proof of submission
  • OpenCalls.fund account, proposal template, declaration of honour, SME declaration and bank-account form
  • Partner letters for pilot sites, municipalities, utilities or industrial hosts

NGI Zero Review - support for existing NGI grantees

Restricted NGI support programme for quality and maturity of digital commons. It is only relevant if the project has already received a grant within the NGI initiative. Services cover security, privacy, accessibility, open-source licensing compliance, standardisation and sustainability of NGI-funded open-source projects.

EIT talent and startup support EIT / EIC InnoNext score 6

InnoNext call for EIT talents and startups

Open EIT/EIC-linked call for fully funded Innovation Internships across Europe. Startups and SMEs can host specialised research talent without financial burden. Eligibility is narrow: startups and SMEs supported by the EIT Community/business-creation services, KIC-supported businesses, KIC innovation partners, or startups/scaleups with at least one EIT Alumni co-founder. Useful if we create an EIT link first.

Rok
2026-07-31
Status
open
Ruta
EIT startup / venture route
Kljucne reci
innonext, eit, eic, innovation internship, startup, sme, talent, no financial burden
Apply

EIT ruta je dobra za startup/pilot/venture podrsku, ali uslovi jako variraju. Prvo proveri PIC, zemlju, starost firme, TRL/prototype, co-funding i da li treba EIT partner.

1. Firma i eligibility

  • Company registration extract: APR for Serbia, MBR for Malta, or equivalent register
  • SME declaration: employees, turnover, balance sheet total, linked/partner enterprises
  • Ownership and UBO structure, with authorised representative details
  • Tax ID, VAT number if applicable, bank account confirmation
  • Short company profile and reference projects
  • PIC number and EU Funding & Tenders organisation registration if requested
  • Proof of startup/SME status, incorporation date, FTE count and ownership/cap table
  • EIT Community link, KIC support, alumni status or partner registration if the call requires it

2. Projekat

  • One-page project concept: problem, solution, target users, expected result
  • Work plan with work packages, milestones, deliverables and timeline
  • Market and impact section: customers, traction, benefits and KPIs
  • Team CVs for key people and role allocation
  • Risk table: technical, commercial, regulatory and delivery risks
  • Pitch deck with problem, solution, TRL/prototype, traction, market and team
  • IP/control evidence for the technology and freedom-to-operate assumptions
  • Pilot or industry-partner challenge statement with validation plan

3. Budzet i finansije

  • Detailed budget by partner and cost category
  • Supplier quotes or cost assumptions for equipment, services and subcontracting
  • Latest financial statements, management accounts or balance sheet
  • State-aid, de minimis and double-funding declarations where requested
  • Cash-flow plan for pre-financing and co-financing
  • Funding-round, co-funding and private-investment evidence where required
  • Cost plan separating grant support, equity/investment support and in-kind partner contribution

4. Partneri i podnosenje

  • Official call text and applicant guide saved locally
  • Eligibility checklist completed before writing the full proposal
  • Authorised signatory decision or power of attorney
  • Submission portal account: EU Login, F6S, national portal or programme portal
  • Final PDF/application package and proof of submission
  • EIT/28DIGITAL/EIT Health/EIT Urban Mobility portal account and call manual saved locally

Open Serbian Innovation Fund AI startup route under the Catalytic co-investing grant programme. It targets micro and small enterprises registered in Serbia, majority-owned by the founding team, up to 10 years old, with an AI prototype and investment contracts ready. 1. Firma i eligibility

  • Company registration extract: APR for Serbia, MBR for Malta, or equivalent register
  • SME declaration: employees, turnover, balance sheet total, linked/partner enterprises
  • Ownership and UBO structure, with authorised representative details
  • Tax ID, VAT number if applicable, bank account confirmation
  • Short company profile and reference projects
  • AJPES / Slovenian Business Register extract for the Slovenian company
  • Slovenian tax number and VAT evidence if applicable
  • Proof of Slovenian establishment, eligible activity and SME status

2. Projekat

  • One-page project concept: problem, solution, target users, expected result
  • Work plan with work packages, milestones, deliverables and timeline
  • Market and impact section: customers, traction, benefits and KPIs
  • Team CVs for key people and role allocation
  • Risk table: technical, commercial, regulatory and delivery risks

3. Budzet i finansije

  • Detailed budget by partner and cost category
  • Supplier quotes or cost assumptions for equipment, services and subcontracting
  • Latest financial statements, management accounts or balance sheet
  • State-aid, de minimis and double-funding declarations where requested
  • Cash-flow plan for pre-financing and co-financing
  • Latest Slovenian annual accounts or interim financial statements
  • Evidence of own contribution or bank/development-bank finance if co-financing is required

4. Partneri i podnosenje

  • Official call text and applicant guide saved locally
  • Eligibility checklist completed before writing the full proposal
  • Authorised signatory decision or power of attorney
  • Submission portal account: EU Login, F6S, national portal or programme portal
  • Final PDF/application package and proof of submission
  • Slovenian national portal account or agency-specific submission account

Status

Ruta

Apply

Ovo je obicno brza SME/voucher ruta. Prvo proveri zemlje koje smeju direktno da apliciraju i da li je bolja Malta ili Slovenija firma.

1. Firma i eligibility

  • Company registration extract: APR for Serbia, MBR for Malta, or equivalent register
  • SME declaration: employees, turnover, balance sheet total, linked/partner enterprises
  • Ownership and UBO structure, with authorised representative details
  • Tax ID, VAT number if applicable, bank account confirmation
  • Short company profile and reference projects
  • Decide lead applicant: Serbia, Malta or Slovenia SME/startup
  • Confirm one-application-per-entity rule before using multiple companies
  • AJPES / Slovenian Business Register extract for the Slovenian company
  • Slovenian tax number and VAT evidence if applicable
  • Proof of Slovenian establishment, eligible activity and SME status
  • SME lead confirmation and partner country eligibility checks
  • NACE/sector fit evidence and SME declaration for the applying company
  • Cluster membership or ecosystem link if the call gives priority to members
  • EU SME eligibility proof and company registration for the applying Malta/Slovenia entity

2. Projekat

  • One-page project concept: problem, solution, target users, expected result
  • Work plan with work packages, milestones, deliverables and timeline
  • Market and impact section: customers, traction, benefits and KPIs
  • Team CVs for key people and role allocation
  • Risk table: technical, commercial, regulatory and delivery risks
  • Select exactly one AID4SME challenge code and align every section to it
  • Write the Annex 2 proposal in the mandatory AID4SME template
  • Define 14-month plan: Plan, Development, Testing & Validation, Assessment
  • Define mandatory deliverables: IP Agreement by M4, Test & Validation Report by M10, Business Plan and Exploitation Roadmap by M14
  • International R&D cooperation plan and partner responsibilities
  • Short voucher use case: problem, service provider, expected output and SME benefit
  • IP protection plan: trade mark, design, patent or IP Scan scope

3. Budzet i finansije

  • Detailed budget by partner and cost category
  • Supplier quotes or cost assumptions for equipment, services and subcontracting
  • Latest financial statements, management accounts or balance sheet
  • State-aid, de minimis and double-funding declarations where requested
  • Cash-flow plan for pre-financing and co-financing
  • Budget for 70% funding rate and maximum EUR 200,000 contribution
  • No subcontracting: keep external work out of the requested project costs
  • Use depreciation only for equipment costs during the project period
  • Latest Slovenian annual accounts or interim financial statements
  • Evidence of own contribution or bank/development-bank finance if co-financing is required
  • Budget split per country according to national funding rules
  • Supplier/service-provider quote and proof that voucher costs are eligible
  • Expected official fees and reimbursement category per voucher type

4. Partneri i podnosenje

  • Official call text and applicant guide saved locally
  • Eligibility checklist completed before writing the full proposal
  • Authorised signatory decision or power of attorney
  • Submission portal account: EU Login, F6S, national portal or programme portal
  • Final PDF/application package and proof of submission
  • Upload final Annex 2 proposal PDF through F6S only
  • Prepare Declaration of Honour, SME Declaration and consortium declaration for contracting if selected
  • Submit before 15 July 2026, 17:00 CEST; do not wait for the final hour
  • Slovenian national portal account or agency-specific submission account
  • Eureka/Eurostars online application and national annexes
  • Cluster Submission Platform or Eurocluster portal account
  • EUIPO account and bank/payment details for reimbursement

  • Quantified environmental or climate impact baseline and target KPIs
  • Pilot/demo site description and permitting or regulatory assumptions
  • Replication and exploitation plan for EU markets
  • Space-enabled value proposition: GNSS, earth observation, satellite communications or space data
  • Data source and technical feasibility note for satellite/space component

3. Budzet i finansije

  • Detailed budget by partner and cost category
  • Supplier quotes or cost assumptions for equipment, services and subcontracting
  • Latest financial statements, management accounts or balance sheet
  • State-aid, de minimis and double-funding declarations where requested
  • Cash-flow plan for pre-financing and co-financing
  • Latest Slovenian annual accounts or interim financial statements
  • Evidence of own contribution or bank/development-bank finance if co-financing is required
  • Supplier/service-provider quote and proof that voucher costs are eligible
  • Co-financing plan, capital-expenditure assumptions and eligible-cost split
  • Costs for data access, integration, validation and field testing

4. Partneri i podnosenje

  • Official call text and applicant guide saved locally
  • Eligibility checklist completed before writing the full proposal
  • Authorised signatory decision or power of attorney
  • Submission portal account: EU Login, F6S, national portal or programme portal
  • Final PDF/application package and proof of submission
  • Slovenian national portal account or agency-specific submission account
  • Cluster Submission Platform or Eurocluster portal account
  • Partner letters for pilot sites, municipalities, utilities or industrial hosts
  • Check ESA delegation / EUSPA / EU eligibility for Malta, Slovenia and Serbia before writing

  • Digital maturity need: AI, cybersecurity, automation, HPC, data or digital transformation gap
  • Test-before-invest plan with expected hub services and pilot outcome
  • Cybersecurity threat model, target users and validation environment
  • Secure-by-design, data protection and compliance assumptions
  • US problem statement and agency fit: NSF, NIH, DOE, NASA, DoD/DIU or ARPA-H
  • Technical innovation narrative with novelty, TRL, milestones and measurable Phase I outcomes
  • Commercialization plan with US customer discovery and letters of support
  • Export-control, data/security and defense-use screening where relevant

3. Budzet i finansije

  • Detailed budget by partner and cost category
  • Supplier quotes or cost assumptions for equipment, services and subcontracting
  • Latest financial statements, management accounts or balance sheet
  • State-aid, de minimis and double-funding declarations where requested
  • Cash-flow plan for pre-financing and co-financing
  • Latest Slovenian annual accounts or interim financial statements
  • Evidence of own contribution or bank/development-bank finance if co-financing is required
  • Estimate internal time and any co-financed service costs
  • Security testing, certification, audit and pilot deployment cost assumptions
  • US budget by labor, consultants, subawards, materials, indirect costs and fee/profit rules
  • Subaward and consultant letters or quotes, especially for university/research partners

  • Authorised signatory decision or power of attorney
  • Submission portal account: EU Login, F6S, national portal or programme portal
  • Final PDF/application package and proof of submission
  • Slovenian national portal account or agency-specific submission account
  • Contact local EDIH hub for Malta, Slovenia or Serbia and request service eligibility
  • Agency portal accounts and deadline calendar for registration steps before proposal submission

Relevant for projects with strong development, sustainability or inclusion impact.

Rok
nije pronadjen
Status
monitoring
Ruta

Kljucne reci

Apply

Otvori zvanicni poziv i prvo potvrdi eligibility, rok, intenzitet finansiranja i obavezne anekse.

1. Firma i eligibility

  • Company registration extract: APR for Serbia, MBR for Malta, or equivalent register
  • SME declaration: employees, turnover, balance sheet total, linked/partner enterprises
  • Ownership and UBO structure, with authorised representative details
  • Tax ID, VAT number if applicable, bank account confirmation
  • Short company profile and reference projects
  • Swedish partner/entity registration and mandate if route requires it

2. Projekat

  • One-page project concept: problem, solution, target users, expected result
  • Work plan with work packages, milestones, deliverables and timeline
  • Market and impact section: customers, traction, benefits and KPIs
  • Team CVs for key people and role allocation
  • Risk table: technical, commercial, regulatory and delivery risks
  • Sustainability, inclusion or international R&D impact narrative

3. Budzet i finansije

  • Detailed budget by partner and cost category
  • Supplier quotes or cost assumptions for equipment, services and subcontracting
  • Latest financial statements, management accounts or balance sheet
  • State-aid, de minimis and double-funding declarations where requested
  • Cash-flow plan for pre-financing and co-financing
  • Swedish partner budget and eligible-cost evidence

4. Partneri i podnosenje

  • Official call text and applicant guide saved locally
  • Eligibility checklist completed before writing the full proposal
  • Authorised signatory decision or power of attorney
  • Submission portal account: EU Login, F6S, national portal or programme portal
  • Final PDF/application package and proof of submission

Ovo je Srbija/UNDP/GEF ruta za lokalne cirkularne projekte. Najbolje radi ako imamo javni interes, lokalnog partnera i merljive ekoloske indikatore.

1. Firma i eligibility

  • SME declaration: employees, turnover, balance sheet total, linked/partner enterprises
  • Ownership and UBO structure, with authorised representative details
  • Tax ID, VAT number if applicable, bank account confirmation
  • Short company profile and reference projects
  • Eligibility evidence for company, NGO, municipality, public utility, research/education body or consortium

2. Projekat

  • One-page project concept: problem, solution, target users, expected result
  • Work plan with work packages, milestones, deliverables and timeline
  • Market and impact section: customers, traction, benefits and KPIs
  • Team CVs for key people and role allocation
  • Risk table: technical, commercial, regulatory and delivery risks

  • Co-financing plan, capital-expenditure assumptions and eligible-cost split

Serbia NGO / EU communication micro-contract EU Delegation to Serbia score 8

EU Values and Policies in Serbia service contract call

Rolling call for Serbian registered associations, CSOs, institutions, foundations, festivals and other entities to deliver civic, cultural, sport, education or intellectual initiatives promoting EU values and policies in Serbia. Proposals are reviewed monthly. Individual service contracts range from EUR 1,500 to EUR 7,000 and can be awarded until the budget is exhausted. Strong fit for the Serbian NGO as dissemination, outreach, event, media or community engagement partner.

Rok
nije pronadjen
Status
rolling
Ruta
Serbia EU communication micro-contract route
Kljucne reci
serbia ngo, eu delegation to serbia, eu values, service contract, dissemination, outreach, events
Apply

Ovo je mikro-ugovor za EU vidljivost, ne klasicni grant. Dobar je za srpski NGO, evente, edukaciju, javnu komunikaciju i dissemination.

1. Firma i eligibility

  • Company registration extract: APR for Serbia, MBR for Malta, or equivalent register
  • SME declaration: employees, turnover, balance sheet total, linked/partner enterprises
  • Ownership and UBO structure, with authorised representative details
  • Tax ID, VAT number if applicable, bank account confirmation
  • Short company profile and reference projects
  • Serbian NGO registration extract, statute and authorised representative evidence
  • Non-profit status, governing bodies and conflict-of-interest declaration
  • References for IT support, training, community outreach or civil society projects
  • Serbian legal registration for NGO, foundation, institution, festival or other eligible entity
  • References for events, public outreach, communication, education or cultural initiatives

2. Projekat

  • One-page project concept: problem, solution, target users, expected result
  • Work plan with work packages, milestones, deliverables and timeline
  • Market and impact section: customers, traction, benefits and KPIs
  • Team CVs for key people and role allocation
  • Risk table: technical, commercial, regulatory and delivery risks
  • Dissemination and communication plan: target groups, channels, events and KPIs
  • Stakeholder/community engagement plan and participant recruitment approach
  • Training/workshop curriculum or digital support methodology
  • Impact narrative for civil society, digital inclusion, media literacy or cyber hygiene
  • Activity concept promoting EU values, policies or Serbia-EU accession topics
  • Target groups, reach, media/social plan and event/workshop delivery plan

3. Budzet i finansije

  • Detailed budget by partner and cost category
  • Supplier quotes or cost assumptions for equipment, services and subcontracting
  • Latest financial statements, management accounts or balance sheet
  • State-aid, de minimis and double-funding declarations where requested
  • Cash-flow plan for pre-financing and co-financing
  • NGO staff time, trainers, communication, events, travel and participant support budget
  • Evidence of co-financing or in-kind contribution if the donor requires it
  • Simple service-contract budget between EUR 1,500 and EUR 7,000

4. Partneri i podnosenje

  • Official call text and applicant guide saved locally
  • Eligibility checklist completed before writing the full proposal
  • Authorised signatory decision or power of attorney
  • Submission portal account: EU Login, F6S, national portal or programme portal
  • Final PDF/application package and proof of submission
  • Partner role letter for the NGO: dissemination, IT support, training or community outreach
  • GDPR/privacy, consent forms and safeguarding policy if working with participants or youth
  • English application form or offer, delivery timeline and visibility plan
  • Post-delivery report template and evidence package for payment after completion
Otvori zvanicni poziv
EIT pre-acceleration / RIS and Malta route EIT Jumpstarter score 8

EIT Jumpstarter 2027 monitoring

EIT Jumpstarter 2026 applications are closed, but it remains a high-value monitoring route for the next edition. 2026 eligibility included Malta, Slovenia and Serbia, with thematic areas including healthcare, food/agritech, raw materials, energy, smart cities/mobility and a Malta-specific agnostic category powered by EIT Communities and Xjenza Malta. Benefits included training, coaching, travel budget and competition for EUR 2,500, EUR 5,000 or EUR 10,000 funding.

EBRD Star Venture monitoring

EBRD startup support route for high-potential ventures in EBRD regions, including advisory, mentoring and ecosystem support rather than a classic EU grant. Useful for Serbia and Western Balkans scaling, especially if paired with investor readiness or market expansion.

Rok
nije pronadjen
Status
monitoring
Ruta
Serbia / Western Balkans
Kljucne reci
ebrd, star venture, startup, western balkans, advisory, scaling, monitoring
Apply

Najverovatnije aplicira srpska firma ili konzorcijum sa Srbijom. Proveri status Srbije u konkretnom programu.

1. Firma i eligibility

  • Company registration extract: APR for Serbia, MBR for Malta, or equivalent register
  • SME declaration: employees, turnover, balance sheet total, linked/partner enterprises
  • Ownership and UBO structure, with authorised representative details
  • Tax ID, VAT number if applicable, bank account confirmation
  • Short company profile and reference projects

2. Projekat

  • One-page project concept: problem, solution, target users, expected result
  • Work plan with work packages, milestones, deliverables and timeline
  • Market and impact section: customers, traction, benefits and KPIs
  • Team CVs for key people and role allocation
  • Risk table: technical, commercial, regulatory and delivery risks

3. Budzet i finansije

  • Detailed budget by partner and cost category
  • Supplier quotes or cost assumptions for equipment, services and subcontracting
  • Latest financial statements, management accounts or balance sheet
  • State-aid, de minimis and double-funding declarations where requested
  • Cash-flow plan for pre-financing and co-financing

4. Partneri i podnosenje

  • Official call text and applicant guide saved locally
  • Eligibility checklist completed before writing the full proposal
  • Authorised signatory decision or power of attorney
  • Submission portal account: EU Login, F6S, national portal or programme portal
  • Final PDF/application package and proof of submission

NATO DIANA challenge monitoring

Transatlantic dual-use accelerator and challenge route for companies from eligible NATO countries. Not an EU grant and not a direct Serbia/Malta route if eligibility is restrictive, but relevant through Slovenia/UK/USA structures or partners if the technology is dual-use and challenge-aligned.

nije pronadjen
Status
monitoring

Kljucne reci

1. Firma i eligibility

  • Company registration extract: APR for Serbia, MBR for Malta, or equivalent register
  • SME declaration: employees, turnover, balance sheet total, linked/partner enterprises
  • Ownership and UBO structure, with authorised representative details
  • Tax ID, VAT number if applicable, bank account confirmation
  • Short company profile and reference projects

  • Slovenian tax number and VAT evidence if applicable
  • Proof of Slovenian establishment, eligible activity and SME status
  • Ownership/control and third-country influence screening

  • SAM.gov registration, UEI and Grants.gov workspace where required
  • Ownership/control memo for SBIR/STTR eligibility, including foreign ownership review
  • Principal Investigator eligibility and employment allocation

2. Projekat

  • One-page project concept: problem, solution, target users, expected result
  • Work plan with work packages, milestones, deliverables and timeline
  • Market and impact section: customers, traction, benefits and KPIs
  • Team CVs for key people and role allocation
  • Risk table: technical, commercial, regulatory and delivery risks
  • Dual-use use case, end-user problem and security-sensitive assumptions
  • Export-control, ITAR/EAR/EU dual-use and classified-information screening
  • US problem statement and agency fit: NSF, NIH, DOE, NASA, DoD/DIU or ARPA-H
  • Technical innovation narrative with novelty, TRL, milestones and measurable Phase I outcomes
  • Commercialization plan with US customer discovery and letters of support
  • Export-control, data/security and defense-use screening where relevant

  • Supplier quotes or cost assumptions for equipment, services and subcontracting
  • Latest financial statements, management accounts or balance sheet
  • State-aid, de minimis and double-funding declarations where requested
  • Cash-flow plan for pre-financing and co-financing
  • Latest Slovenian annual accounts or interim financial statements
  • Evidence of own contribution or bank/development-bank finance if co-financing is required
  • Prototype/test budget and defence customer validation assumptions
  • US budget by labor, consultants, subawards, materials, indirect costs and fee/profit rules
  • Subaward and consultant letters or quotes, especially for university/research partners

  • Eligibility checklist completed before writing the full proposal
  • Authorised signatory decision or power of attorney
  • Submission portal account: EU Login, F6S, national portal or programme portal
  • Final PDF/application package and proof of submission
  • Slovenian national portal account or agency-specific submission account
  • Security and eligibility review before sharing sensitive technical details
  • Agency portal accounts and deadline calendar for registration steps before proposal submission

New European Bauhaus funding opportunities monitoring

EU route for projects at the intersection of sustainability, inclusion, design, built environment, culture and community. Useful for smart buildings, urban tech, community pilots, sustainability storytelling and NGO dissemination around green/digital projects.

Rok
nije pronadjen
Status
monitoring
Ruta
EU creative / NEB route
Kljucne reci
new european bauhaus, sustainability, design, built environment, community, funding
Apply

Koristi samo ako imamo realan creative, culture, design, sustainability ili community angle, najbolje sa NGO/creative partnerima.

1. Firma i eligibility

  • Company registration extract: APR for Serbia, MBR for Malta, or equivalent register
  • SME declaration: employees, turnover, balance sheet total, linked/partner enterprises
  • Ownership and UBO structure, with authorised representative details
  • Tax ID, VAT number if applicable, bank account confirmation
  • Short company profile and reference projects

2. Projekat

  • One-page project concept: problem, solution, target users, expected result
  • Work plan with work packages, milestones, deliverables and timeline
  • Market and impact section: customers, traction, benefits and KPIs
  • Team CVs for key people and role allocation
  • Risk table: technical, commercial, regulatory and delivery risks
  • Creative, cultural or New European Bauhaus narrative: sustainability, inclusion and design quality
  • Audience/community engagement and dissemination concept with NGO or creative partners

3. Budzet i finansije

  • Detailed budget by partner and cost category
  • Supplier quotes or cost assumptions for equipment, services and subcontracting
  • Latest financial statements, management accounts or balance sheet
  • State-aid, de minimis and double-funding declarations where requested
  • Cash-flow plan for pre-financing and co-financing
  • Content, design, events, communication and creative partner budget lines

4. Partneri i podnosenje

  • Official call text and applicant guide saved locally
  • Eligibility checklist completed before writing the full proposal
  • Authorised signatory decision or power of attorney
  • Submission portal account: EU Login, F6S, national portal or programme portal
  • Final PDF/application package and proof of submission
  • Portfolio, demo or visual evidence for the creative/design component

CHIST-ERA ICT and emerging technologies calls monitoring

Apply

1. Firma i eligibility

  • Company registration extract: APR for Serbia, MBR for Malta, or equivalent register
  • SME declaration: employees, turnover, balance sheet total, linked/partner enterprises
  • Ownership and UBO structure, with authorised representative details
  • Tax ID, VAT number if applicable, bank account confirmation
  • Short company profile and reference projects
  • National funding eligibility check for every partner country and funding agency

2. Projekat

  • One-page project concept: problem, solution, target users, expected result
  • Work plan with work packages, milestones, deliverables and timeline
  • Market and impact section: customers, traction, benefits and KPIs
  • Team CVs for key people and role allocation
  • Risk table: technical, commercial, regulatory and delivery risks
  • Transnational R&I concept with research question, pilot path and partner roles
  • Cybersecurity threat model, target users and validation environment

  • Detailed budget by partner and cost category
  • Supplier quotes or cost assumptions for equipment, services and subcontracting
  • Latest financial statements, management accounts or balance sheet
  • State-aid, de minimis and double-funding declarations where requested
  • Cash-flow plan for pre-financing and co-financing
  • Budget aligned to each national or regional funding agency's rules
  • Security testing, certification, audit and pilot deployment cost assumptions

4. Partneri i podnosenje

  • Official call text and applicant guide saved locally
  • Eligibility checklist completed before writing the full proposal
  • Authorised signatory decision or power of attorney

  • Final PDF/application package and proof of submission
  • Pre-proposal/full-proposal timeline and partner commitment letters

COST Open Call networking route monitoring

nije pronadjen

  • SME declaration: employees, turnover, balance sheet total, linked/partner enterprises
  • Ownership and UBO structure, with authorised representative details
  • Tax ID, VAT number if applicable, bank account confirmation
  • Short company profile and reference projects

EU finance / funds and guarantees EIF score 6

European Investment Fund SME finance route

EIF does not usually fund SMEs directly, but backs venture funds, guarantees and intermediaries. Important radar for finding EU-backed VC, debt, guarantees and financial intermediaries in Malta, Slovenia and nearby markets.

Rok
nije pronadjen
Status
monitoring
Ruta
EU finance route
Kljucne reci
eif, sme finance, venture capital, guarantees, intermediaries, eu finance
Apply

Ovo nije klasicni grant. Pripremi investment case, finansije i dokaz rasta; koristi kao sloj finansiranja uz grantove.

1. Firma i eligibility

  • Company registration extract: APR for Serbia, MBR for Malta, or equivalent register
  • SME declaration: employees, turnover, balance sheet total, linked/partner enterprises
  • Ownership and UBO structure, with authorised representative details
  • Tax ID, VAT number if applicable, bank account confirmation
  • Short company profile and reference projects
  • AJPES / Slovenian Business Register extract for the Slovenian company
  • Slovenian tax number and VAT evidence if applicable
  • Proof of Slovenian establishment, eligible activity and SME status
  • US entity formation plan: C-Corp or LLC, EIN, bank account and accounting setup
  • SAM.gov registration, UEI and Grants.gov workspace where required
  • Ownership/control memo for SBIR/STTR eligibility, including foreign ownership review
  • Principal Investigator eligibility and employment allocation

2. Projekat

  • One-page project concept: problem, solution, target users, expected result
  • Work plan with work packages, milestones, deliverables and timeline
  • Market and impact section: customers, traction, benefits and KPIs
  • Team CVs for key people and role allocation
  • Risk table: technical, commercial, regulatory and delivery risks
  • Investment case: market, traction, pipeline, growth plan and EU impact
  • US problem statement and agency fit: NSF, NIH, DOE, NASA, DoD/DIU or ARPA-H
  • Technical innovation narrative with novelty, TRL, milestones and measurable Phase I outcomes
  • Commercialization plan with US customer discovery and letters of support
  • Export-control, data/security and defense-use screening where relevant

3. Budzet i finansije

  • Detailed budget by partner and cost category
  • Supplier quotes or cost assumptions for equipment, services and subcontracting
  • Latest financial statements, management accounts or balance sheet
  • State-aid, de minimis and double-funding declarations where requested
  • Cash-flow plan for pre-financing and co-financing
  • Latest Slovenian annual accounts or interim financial statements
  • Evidence of own contribution or bank/development-bank finance if co-financing is required
  • Financial model, runway, debt capacity, cap table and fundraising history
  • Use of funds and co-financing sources
  • US budget by labor, consultants, subawards, materials, indirect costs and fee/profit rules
  • Subaward and consultant letters or quotes, especially for university/research partners

4. Partneri i podnosenje

  • Official call text and applicant guide saved locally
  • Eligibility checklist completed before writing the full proposal
  • Authorised signatory decision or power of attorney
  • Submission portal account: EU Login, F6S, national portal or programme portal
  • Final PDF/application package and proof of submission
  • Slovenian national portal account or agency-specific submission account
  • Investor data room: deck, financials, contracts, IP, legal and references
  • Agency portal accounts and deadline calendar for registration steps before proposal submission

Innovation Centre Denmark funding and partner route monitoring

Organizer route behind The DeepTechers. Useful if we build a Denmark partner route, especially through Copenhagen, DTU, life science, tech, green transition or US/Israel/Asia links.

Global startup cloud credits AWS Activate score 5

AWS Activate startup credits monitoring

Organizer route behind The DeepTechers. AWS Activate is not a cash grant, but eligible startups can apply for cloud promotional credits: self-funded startups up to USD 5,000 and pre-Series B portfolio startups up to USD 200,000, with larger AI startup credits by invitation. Use only as infrastructure support, not as replacement for the Microsoft-stack build.
